## <a name="windows-server-2012-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="2aa7c-1912">Attributs Windows Server 2012</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2aa7c-1912">Windows Server 2012 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="2aa7c-1913">Cette classe contient les attributs suivants pour Windows Server 2012 :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="2aa7c-1913">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2012:</span></span>
